class _h {
    _language = "en";
    constructor() {
        this.detectLanguage()
    }
    detectLanguage() {
        try {
            const E = Eh.i18n.getUILanguage();
            this._language = E.startsWith("zh") ? "zh" : "en"
        } catch {
            this._language = navigator.language.startsWith("zh") ? "zh" : "en",
            console.warn(" browser.i18n API navigator.language")
        }
    }
    setLanguage(E) {
        this._language = E === "zh" ? "zh" : "en"
    }
    getLanguage() {
        return this._language
    }
    translate(E, _) {
        return Cm[E] ? Cm[E][this._language] || _ || E : (console.warn(`Missing translation for key: ${E}`),
        _ || E)
    }
    t(E, _) {
        return this.translate(E, _)
    }
}
